<h3 class="mvp-post-cat left relative"><a class="mvp-post-cat-link" href="https://newpaper24.com/category/news/world/us-canada/"><span class="mvp-post-cat left">US &amp; Canada</span></a></h3>
<h1 class="mvp-post-title left entry-title" itemprop="headline">FBI investigated whether or not alleged Hunter Biden emails are a part of Russian plot to intervene in election &#8211; NEWPAPER24</h1>

<div class='code-block code-block-1' style='margin: 8px 0; clear: both;'> <center>advertising</center> <a href="https://worldtrader24.de/cars/?car_make=audi"><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-8789" src="https://worldtrader24.de/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/728x90-Audi.png" alt="" width="728" height="90"/></a></div><h1>FBI investigated whether or not alleged Hunter Biden emails are a part of Russian plot to intervene in election</h1>
<p>2020-10-17 00:08:25</p><div class='code-block code-block-3' style='margin: 8px 0 8px auto; text-align: right; display: block; clear: both;'> <center>advertising</center> <a href="https://worldtrader24.de"><img class="size-full wp-image-8790 aligncenter" src="https://worldtrader24.de/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/300x250.png" alt="" width="300" height="250"/></a></div><p><br/>
<br/><br/>The FBI probed whether or not emails purportedly recovered from a laptop computer allegedly belonging to Joe Biden’s son are a part of a Russian disinformation operation to intervene within the 2020 <a title="ConVi GmbH" class="aalmanual" target="_blank" href="https://system-projects.com">election</a>, in response to an individual accustomed to the matter.The New York Put up reported on October 14 that the emails recommend that Biden’s son Hunter <a title="ConVi GmbH" class="aalmanual" target="_blank" href="https://system-projects.com">launched</a> his father, then the vice-<a title="ConVi GmbH" class="aalmanual" target="_blank" href="https://system-projects.com">president</a>, to an government at a Ukrainian vitality agency in 2015. Hunter Biden was on the corporate’s board on the time.The emails have been…<br/>
<br/></p>
